  <span id="freeText18326132983091685934" style="display:none"><blockquote>
  <b>⋰⋱⋰⋱⋰⋱*Fuck me. Not in a good way*⋰⋱⋰⋱⋰⋱</b>
</blockquote> <br><b>
  <u>Re-read: 31.01.2018</u>
</b><br>This was a better re-read than #2 and #3, it was still not as I remembered. My love for this series just isn't there anymore and it sucks big time. I remember LOVING this series. Loving Merit and loving Ethan to death. Now... I love Ethan, and like the rest. However, I'm missing the adoration I had for the character. For Ethan. I always thought of Ethan as powerful, but everyone keeps being strong and more powerful than him. Including Merit and Gabriel. Hell, I'm even imagining what things would be like if Gabriel was Merit's love interest. I'm nuts.<br><br><b><u>The characters</u>:</b><br>— <b>Caroline ‘Merit’ ‘Mer’ Merit</b> (becomes vampire at 27, but is 28 in years), Sentinel of the Cadogan House.<br>— <b>Ethan ‘Liege’ ‘Darth Sullivan’ Sullivan</b> (394, though became a vampire at 30), master of the Cadogan House.<br>—<b>Mallory ‘Mal’ Delancey Carmichael</b>, Merit's bestfriend and a fourth-class sorcerer, a master of the First Key; power.<br>— <b>Charles ‘Chuck’ Merit</b>, Merit's grandfather is the Ombudsman; a ‘liaison’ between the regulars and the sups.<br>— Chuck's team: his secretary, <b>Marjorie</b> (50) (though we haven't met her), the computer prodigy and a shape-shifter, <b> Jeffrey ‘Jeff’ Christopher</b> (21), and a fourth-class sorcerer, <b>Catcher Bell</b> (29). There's also a Housed vampire who works for him that not even his colleagues knows about.<br>— <b>Joshua Merit</b>, Merit's dad sucky dad.<br>— guard of the Cadogan House, <b>Lindsey</b> (115) and who is also a psychic, and a good friend to Merit.<br>— <b>Lucas ‘Luc’</b>, the head of Cadogan House’s guard corps.<br>— <b>Morgan Greer</b>, now Master of Navarre House, (72, though looks 28) Merit's sorta ex.<br>— <b>Gabriel ‘Gabe’ Keene</b>, Apex of the Central North American, Jeff's pack leader (love him).<br>— <b>Darius West</b>, head of the Greenwich Presidium and a total dick.<br>— <b>Seth Tate</b> (36), the mayor of Chicago and a fucker.<br>— <b>Scott Grey</b>, Master of Grey House.<br>— <b>Noah Beck</b>, the leader of Chicago’s independent vampires and a Red Guard ‘RG’ (a vampire Secret Service, of sorts).<br>— <b>Jonah</b>, the Guard Captain, Grey House and a Red Guard.<br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>“You can run. You can keep running to the ends of the earth. But I won’t be far behind you.”</i>

<div id="review_1084731015" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1084731015" />
    <a title="Chelsea ❤Peril Please❤ " class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/8422853-chelsea-peril-please"><img alt="Chelsea ❤Peril Please❤ " src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1570038444p2/8422853.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1084731015?book_show_action=true">Oct 20, 2014</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Chelsea ❤Peril Please❤ " class="user" itemprop="url" name="Chelsea ❤Peril Please❤ " href="/user/show/8422853-chelsea-peril-please">Chelsea ❤Peril Please❤ </a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/8422853-chelsea-peril-please?shelf=could-read-over-and-over-again">could-read-over-and-over-again</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/8422853-chelsea-peril-please?shelf=serious-cliffhanger">serious-cliffhanger</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/8422853-chelsea-peril-please?shelf=tearjerkers">tearjerkers</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/8422853-chelsea-peril-please?shelf=unforgettable-male-leads">unforgettable-male-leads</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/8422853-chelsea-peril-please?shelf=don-t-be-fooled-by-the-cover">don-t-be-fooled-by-the-cover</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/8422853-chelsea-peril-please?shelf=awesome-heroines">awesome-heroines</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/8422853-chelsea-peril-please?shelf=favorites">favorites</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1084731015" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer16620747273760170102"><b>*4.5 stars*</b><br/><br/><b>
  <i>…he stroked my jawline with his thumb. “You can run. You can keep running to the ends of the earth. But I won’t be far behind you.”</i>
</b><br/><br/>Oh. My. God. Really?? <i>Reeeeaallyyy??</i> Ugh, that was a low blow. It’s not that I didn’t think this would inevitably happen in one of these books, it’s more that I didn’t expect it to happen <i>so early.</i> It was <b>epic</b>, amazing….unexpected. It was everything I’ve wanted from my latest obsession (cough, Ethan, cough), but everything that could bring my world cra</span>
  <span id="freeText16620747273760170102" style="display:none"><b>*4.5 stars*</b><br><br><b>
  <i>…he stroked my jawline with his thumb. “You can run. You can keep running to the ends of the earth. But I won’t be far behind you.”</i>
</b><br><br>Oh. My. God. Really?? <i>Reeeeaallyyy??</i> Ugh, that was a low blow. It’s not that I didn’t think this would inevitably happen in one of these books, it’s more that I didn’t expect it to happen <i>so early.</i> It was <b>epic</b>, amazing….unexpected. It was everything I’ve wanted from my latest obsession (cough, Ethan, cough), but everything that could bring my world crashing to the ground in a burning heap of perished dreams. <br><br>It’s been a few days since I finished this book, so the emotions I felt upon finishing in my sleep-deprived state have long since vanished, leaving only a hollow, dull ache where my heart should be. I asked for the peril, I asked for something wicked and jaw-dropping to happen, and it did. Go figure-an author actually did what I asked, but made it <b>better.</b> Not often do my evil wishes get granted, but it seems that when they do, they are granted full-force, causing me to lose my breath in what can only be an indignant, albeit shocked, gasp. <br><br>This world has captured me-stolen my heart and made it impossible to breathe without one of the installments firmly within my grasp. Even as I read an absolute favorite of mine, I felt my thoughts swirling together and convoluting what was happening within each novel-that’s a feat I don’t take lightly. <br>I’m sorry, guys, but Ethan has shown his true colors. He is just….perfection. I <b>adore</b> this hulking man-vamp. He made a fatal error in the last book (Okay, actually, he made a devastating <b>mistake</b>, let’s change that last phrase in light of recent events) and he is truly trying his hardest to make up for it. It was precious, sweet…..not words that I suppose generally apply to vampires, much less God damn Ethan Sullivan, but he’s <i>trying.</i> Maybe he is still that up-tight, pretentious boss that all of Cadogan House love to make fun of, but he’s becoming more human each and every day-he’s saying things that make my heart melt into a puddle of goo and he’s making proclamations that can only be described as someone who has fallen madly in love….and it’s all because of <b>Merit.</b><br><br><b>”Ethan-“<br>“No. I will never be far behind you.” He tipped up my chin so that I could do nothing else but look back into his eyes. “Do the things you need to do. Learn to be a vampire, to be a warrior, to be the soldier you are capable of being. But consider the possibility that I made a mistake I regret-and that I’ll continue to regret that mistake and try to convince you to give me another chance until the earth stops turning.”</b><br><br>Merit, still nursing her wounds from the saddening events from the previous novel, is stubborn and fierce as ever. She’s a force to be reckoned with and is strengthening herself so she can protect the house and it’s master under any and all circumstances. I understand her heart is broken, oh my god, do I get it…..but poor, poor Ethan. He really did screw up, that’s for sure. A job before a girl you think you love?? Not fair-but, again, he did what he thought was best for the house, and, even though he still loves Cadogan House, he realizes there’s something about companionship , and let’s face it, Merit, he can’t live without. He’s lived centuries without love or someone to laugh and/or relax with, and in comes Merit breaking his carefully sculpted mold. It’s understandable, to me, that he was nervous of what he might do to protect the girl he loves so he made what he thought was a smart decision, a decision that he regrets every day.<br><br><b>My stomach growled at the smells; there was only so much blocking that a vampire could do. I silently promised myself a deep-fried candy bar and a paper tray of bacon-wrapped Tator Tots if I made it through the night unscathed. Not a good nutritional combo, but I figured the odds were low anyway.</b><br><br>The thing is, I love Merit. She really never does wrong in my eyes-selfless, fierce, loyal, loves with all her heart even as she has her guard up-what’s not to like?? So I didn’t roll my eyes when she ignored his advances and I didn’t get mad when she didn’t just take him back-she’s a great character. But, there’s so much more to it than that. In this book, because they aren’t physically involved (technicality), they have connected on a much deeper, more visceral level. It’s hard to say that she doesn’t see or feel that. I just hope…well, what the fuck? What does it matter what I hope-if wishes were fishes, we’d all throw nets, right? <br><br>I can’t say what I hope or wish or feel, because it would spoil what <i>is.</i> But, I refuse to believe it, so I guess you all need to read to see if you believe or not, that this is real. No way. I guess that’s why I’m just sitting back, tapping my fingers on my desk, pondering, waiting for the inevitable prestige…if you get what I’m sayin’. <br><br><a href="http://s1301.photobucket.com/user/ChelseaRoberts3/media/cookie-monster-waiting_zpssod1vn7o.gif.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1414075426ra/11604770.gif" alt=" photo cookie-monster-waiting_zpssod1vn7o.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br><br><br><br><br><i>For more of my reviews, please visit:</i><br><a href="http://starcrossedbookblog.com/chelsea/" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img height="200" width="320" src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1491628712i/22430034._SX540_.jpg" alt="descriptive text here" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a> <u>
  <b></b>
</u><br><a href="http://starcrossedbookblog.com/chelsea/%20" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img height="60" width="139" src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1409285880i/10960212.jpg" alt="descriptive text here" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a> <u>
  <b></b>
</u><br><br><br><br><br><br><br>****************<b>4.5 stars</b><br><br>Oh. My. GOD. That. ending.....<b>it destroyed me.</b><br><br>I'll write a review when I can but....ooooooh the feels. <br><br>♥Ethan-I LOVE YOU.</span>

<div id="review_128080476" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/128080476" />
    <a title="Francesca the Fierce (Under the Covers Book Blog)" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/3108364-francesca-the-fierce-under-the-covers-book-blog"><img alt="Francesca the Fierce (Under the Covers Book Blog)" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1595947372p2/3108364.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/128080476?book_show_action=true">Oct 26, 2010</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Francesca the Fierce (Under the Covers Book Blog)" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Francesca the Fierce (Under the Covers Book Blog)" href="/user/show/3108364-francesca-the-fierce-under-the-covers-book-blog">Francesca the Fierce (Under the Covers Book Blog)</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3108364-francesca-the-fierce-under-the-covers-book-blog?shelf=read-audio-books">read-audio-books</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3108364-francesca-the-fierce-under-the-covers-book-blog?shelf=vampires">vampires</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3108364-francesca-the-fierce-under-the-covers-book-blog?shelf=genre-urban-fantasy">genre-urban-fantasy</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3108364-francesca-the-fierce-under-the-covers-book-blog?shelf=books-read-2011">books-read-2011</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3108364-francesca-the-fierce-under-the-covers-book-blog?shelf=witches-shaman-magic">witches-shaman-magic</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3108364-francesca-the-fierce-under-the-covers-book-blog?shelf=werewolves-shifters">werewolves-shifters</a>
          </div>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer128080476" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer12843267621818236362">This review was posted at <a href='http://underthecoversbookblog.blogspot.com/2011/05/review-hard-bitten-by-chloe-neill.html' rel='nofollow noopener'>Under The Covers</a><br/><br/>Chicago is in a bit of an uproar against vampires, who are being accused of murdering humans at raves. Ethan has a warrant for his arrest out from the CPD. Cadogan House is still under repairs. Humans are protesting outside the House.<br/><br/>Merit is now forced to investigate these human murders to clear Ethan's name, using Jonah as an ally, they try to infiltrate the raves to gather information, and stumble upon a drug that is making vampires crazy and brings o</span>
  <span id="freeText12843267621818236362" style="display:none">This review was posted at <a href="http://underthecoversbookblog.blogspot.com/2011/05/review-hard-bitten-by-chloe-neill.html" rel="nofollow noopener">Under The Covers</a><br /><br />Chicago is in a bit of an uproar against vampires, who are being accused of murdering humans at raves. Ethan has a warrant for his arrest out from the CPD. Cadogan House is still under repairs. Humans are protesting outside the House.<br /><br />Merit is now forced to investigate these human murders to clear Ethan's name, using Jonah as an ally, they try to infiltrate the raves to gather information, and stumble upon a drug that is making vampires crazy and brings out all their violent trades.<br /><br />As usual with Chicagoland Vampires, there's a lot of vampire politics and intrigue in this book. We still see the usual suspects, Jeff, Catcher, Mallory. Mallory is actually going through a bit of an identity and adaptation crisis, but it's nice to see Merit being there for her. Catcher, can I just say... Now with the glasses we could just use him as a role play fantasy of a naughty professor ;) Lindsey and Luc and their relationship or lack of. And I just really like Jonah, I want to read more about him!<br /><br />One complaint I do have, "V". Why the name? I mean if we really had to go there with the storyline, which take a bit of an idea from <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/715791.Kiss_of_Crimson__Midnight_Breed___2_" title="Kiss of Crimson (Midnight Breed, #2) by Lara Adrian" rel="nofollow noopener">Kiss of Crimson</a>, why call it V as it has been used before as well? True Blood anyone?<br /><br />I really didn't see the bad guy at the end coming, the sneaky bastard! And, yes, let's face it, I have to talk about the end. How could one little part of a book now have become the only thing I can remember happening in the whole book?!?!? I don't want to spoil what happens, yes you should be scared of it. It will probably have you crying. <br /><br />Oh.My.God! I really didn't see it coming. I feel like my heart has been ripped out of my chest. And yes, I'm crying! How could Ms. Neill do this to us? I really had hopes, and then... OK, I'll try to have faith, even though I don't see a way to fix this now. *pass me a tissue so I can finish typing this review*. I don't think I can take anymore heartache from this series, and I really hope next book has a resolution in sigh, a HAPPY one. November just feels so far away now, I wish I would've waited.<br /><br /><b>Favorite Quotes:</b><br /><br /><blockquote>
  <i>"You wouldn't say that if he was making you levitate a 200 pound lead weight for the 67th time" - Mallory</i>
</blockquote><br /><br /><blockquote>
  <i>"You can run. You can keep running to the ends of the earth. But I won’t be far behind you."<br />"Ethan—"<br />"No. I will never be far behind you.” He tipped up my chin so that I could do nothing else but look back into his eyes. “Do the things you need to do. Learn to be a vampire, to be a warrior, to be the soldier you are capable of being. But consider the possibility that I made a mistake I regret—and that I’ll continue to regret that mistake and try to convince you to give me another chance until the earth stops turning." </i>
</blockquote><br /><br /><blockquote>
  <i>"No one said love was easy, Sentinel." - Ethan</i>
</blockquote><br /><br /><b>Again with the damn crying!</b></span>

<div id="review_1069868227" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1069868227" />
    <a title="✘✘ Sarah ✘✘ (former Nefarious Breeder of Murderous Crustaceans)" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/7298986-sarah-former-nefarious-breeder-of-murderous-crustaceans"><img alt="✘✘ Sarah ✘✘ (former Nefarious Breeder of Murderous Crustaceans)" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1587115780p2/7298986.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1069868227?book_show_action=true">Oct 02, 2014</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="✘✘ Sarah ✘✘ (former Nefarious Breeder of Murderous Crustaceans)" class="user" itemprop="url" name="✘✘ Sarah ✘✘ (former Nefarious Breeder of Murderous Crustaceans)" href="/user/show/7298986-sarah-former-nefarious-breeder-of-murderous-crustaceans">✘✘ Sarah ✘✘ (former Nefarious Breeder of Murderous Crustaceans)</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="Kindle Edition " href="/book/show/11101753-hard-bitten">review of another edition</a>


        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/7298986-sarah-former-nefarious-breeder-of-murderous-crustaceans?shelf=2014">2014</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/7298986-sarah-former-nefarious-breeder-of-murderous-crustaceans?shelf=urban-fantasy">urban-fantasy</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/7298986-sarah-former-nefarious-breeder-of-murderous-crustaceans?shelf=vamps-are-wimps">vamps-are-wimps</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1069868227" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer12016036542309131306">When I started reading Hard Bitten I already knew what was coming at the end of the instalment. I’d read many reviews for both this book and the next and had guessed the outcome. Shock, disbelief, dismay: I went through it all before I even got my hands on Hard Bitten. Now, being aware of what would happen didn’t make it any less heartbreaking when it did. I just finished reading the book, my stomach is in knots and I feel like I’ve been sucker-punched. <br/><br/>Now this was one gutsy move on Chloe Neill</span>
  <span id="freeText12016036542309131306" style="display:none">When I started reading Hard Bitten I already knew what was coming at the end of the instalment. I’d read many reviews for both this book and the next and had guessed the outcome. Shock, disbelief, dismay: I went through it all before I even got my hands on Hard Bitten. Now, being aware of what would happen didn’t make it any less heartbreaking when it did. I just finished reading the book, my stomach is in knots and I feel like I’ve been sucker-punched. <br /><br />Now this was one gutsy move on Chloe Neill’s part. As hard as it is to accept, I actually understand why she might have opted for such a drastic plot twist. <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[First, I don’t know how Merit &amp; Ethan’s relationship could have evolved hadn’t Ethan died. A perfectly happy ending wouldn’t have been satisfying (there’s no fun in that, especially not for these two) and neither would have a “love you-love you not” status quo between Sentinel and Master, which would have become boring really fast. Ethan’s death is heartbreaking but it does make sense somehow. Second, the Red Guard thing. Ever since the RG came into the equation I felt that joining them should be Merit’s next move, it would be so… Merit really. Of course she couldn’t do so without betraying Ethan but now that he is gone I can see her becoming an RG. That would be an interesting direction for this series to take. I guess I will have to wait and see what happens in the next few instalments <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span> I’ve read quite a few reviews complaining about the way Neill handled the scene in question but I thought it was just perfect: sudden, unexpected, over in a second. Like Merit, the reader doesn’t see it coming. Neill couldn’t have done it better. I also disagree with those who tax Neill with “emotionless writing.” It’s just the opposite for me: this whole series is such an emotional roller-coaster that each instalment pretty much leaves me exhausted! <br /><br />I have to admit that the first part of the book wasn’t as fast-paced as previous instalments but it was still highly enjoyable, with lots of twists and turns. I just love Merit and she keeps growing on me with each new instalment. Ethan makes me melt (that scene when he is alone with Merit in his office had me drooling all along). I love Lindsey (much) more than I do Mallory. I love Luc. Darius is an asshole. Tate is an asshole. Morgan is an asshole. We get to see a bit more of Scott Grey and I think I’m beginning to like him quite a bit. We get to see A LOT more of Jonah. <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[Now, it definitely feels like Neill is prepping us for some Merit-Jonah action in instalments to come. I’m not sure when it will happen but I’m pretty sure it will. What bothered me here was that Neill was too obvious about it. Then again, I might be completely wrong about this. <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span> All in all, great characterization as always. <br /><br />And… I finally got answers to two questions that had been bugging me since the first instalment in the series: why Ethan happened to be on the campus grounds the night Merit was attacked and why Merit goes by Merit instead of Caroline.<br /><br />Hard Bitten is a fantastic, emotionally draining read. Getting my hands on Drink Deep right NOW!<br /><br /><i>ETA: Just finished reading Drink Deep. Pretty much speechless. Definitely giddy. Chloe Neill, you evil, evil woman. You really got me there!!</i></span>
  <a data-text-id="12016036542309131306" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

  <div class="left bodycol">

              <span id="reviewTextContainer99372185" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer5870092636395765591"><b> I really disliked the ending.</b> Not the whole book, but the ending killed all my fascination with the series. I would've rated it higher but I just can't with an ending like this one. The book was great but when something as big as this happens right at the end it changes everything. These are <b>the reasons</b> for why I am completely against this book:<br/><br/><a class='jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction'>(view spoiler)</a><span class='spoilerContainer' style='display: none'>[<br/>1)<b> You just don't kill the freaking hero. </b> He did change, he did love and tresure Merit, so why kill him, Chloe Neill? I really did cry w</span></span>
  <span id="freeText5870092636395765591" style="display:none"><b> I really disliked the ending.</b> Not the whole book, but the ending killed all my fascination with the series. I would've rated it higher but I just can't with an ending like this one. The book was great but when something as big as this happens right at the end it changes everything. These are <b>the reasons</b> for why I am completely against this book:<br /><br /><a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[<br />1)<b> You just don't kill the freaking hero. </b> He did change, he did love and tresure Merit, so why kill him, Chloe Neill? I really did cry with the ending. He dyed protecting her, *sigh, so tragic. You dont make us all adore Ethan and then kill him from one second to the next! For 3 whole books Ethan had always been the total center of my attention and now he is gone, how am I suppose to just let something like that go? I just think it's never gonna be the same for me now. To revive him won't work, he just never should have dyed in the first place... I'm so frustrated right now! I was completely having an amazing time and then this terrible ending ruined everything for me! <br /><br />2) Even worse, this book only made me realize this two characters (Merit and Ethan) were totally perfect for each other and I just know no one else will work for her. So what now!?I just don't see things being ok without him. <b>Everything was about him. </b> Merit may have been the heroine but most of her thoughts were about him, most of her actions were done thinking in how he would react. <br /><br />3) <b>Did Merit had to get over him so fast? Really? </b>I mean the guy died trying to protect her after she completely slapped his love declaration on his face and distrusted him. He did everything he could to show her how much he truly loved her and he really tried to make amends but she still kept rejecting him over and over again, haven't you ever heard of 2nd chances honey? I guess you will be regretting that now, wont you? **Sigh, I really don't think I will be ok with a new love interest.<br /><br />Aghhhhhhhh<br /><br />Chloe Neill I truly hope you had have enough time thinking in a way to fix this total <s>screw up!</s> mess. I really can't, so I hope your imagination is stronger than mine because I'm totally getting off this series if Ethan won't be on it anymore. I do have faith, though, that you will fix this.<br /><br /> <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span><br /><br />Now for those of you who want something from me which is not a spoiler know that I'm glad I waited to read this book because I probably would have abandonded the series if it wasn't because I now know next book is already out and things will eventually get back as they should. If I had to wait a whole year after this tragic ending I don't think I would be strong enough to keep reading. Don't get me wrong, I loved the rest of the books and I KNOW things will get better again, but the shock of what happened was too much for me.<br /><br />How could you guys rate this book with 5 stars?? Know that all of those who did completely broke my heart. I love this author too guys, but this book crossed the line IMHO.How can you be ok with something like this happening? It may get better in the next books but the rating is about this one. How could you rate with 5 stars a book with an ending like this one? It's ok for an author to search ways to impact and shock their audience but I believe there are some limits that should never be crossed. <br /><br /><br /></span>

  function submitShelfLink(unique_id, book_id, shelf_id, shelf_name, submit_form, exclusive) {
    var checkbox_id = 'shelf_name_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    var element = document.getElementById(checkbox_id)

    var checked = element.checked
    if (checked && exclusive) {
      // can't uncheck a radio by clicking it!
      return
    }
    if(document.getElementById("savingMessage")){
      Element.show('savingMessage')
    }
    var element_id = 'shelfInDropdownName_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    Element.update(element_id, "saving...");
    if (submit_form) {
      Element.hide('shelfDropdown_' + unique_id)
      var form = document.getElementById('addBookForm' + book_id)
      if (form) {
        form.shelf.value = shelf_name
        form.onsubmit()
      }
    }
    else {
      var action = checked ? 'remove' : ''
      element.checked = !element.checked
      new Ajax.Request('/shelf/add_to_shelf', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name)}, parameters:'book_id=' + book_id + '&name=' + shelf_name + '&a=' + action + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('Ff/meQr+3ZBWVIHgB2a+bdxT/A/iBEwePUvM5Gn4PNyLECeMmwqZqh6udVxYhBrbxwgkCiqjJSB7xUfJx4rguQ==')})
    }
  }

  function shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name) {
    Element.update('shelfListfalse_' + book_id, request.responseText)
    afterShelfSave(checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name.escapeHTML())
  }

  function refreshGroupBox(group_id, book_id) {
    new Ajax.Updater('addGroupBooks' + book_id + '', '/group/add_book_box', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){refreshGroupBoxComplete(request, book_id);}, parameters:'id=' + group_id + '&book_id=' + book_id + '&refresh=true' + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('OTJRm/FDdjI859pXNnjcpo1YGfC9KRjARW0AgWQGjwyn3ZBuYLcyCHQdLutpmngQlgPB9XWOcf4D44usynRTaQ==')})
  }
